				<content:encoded><![CDATA[<img width="300" height="145" src="http://coverville.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/cov1163-300x145.jpg" class="attachment-medium size-medium wp-post-image" alt="" srcset="http://coverville.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/cov1163-300x145.jpg 300w, http://coverville.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/cov1163.jpg 620w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" /><p>Got your late-80s/early-90&#8217;s hat on? How about your shoes? Suspenders? I don&#8217;t know, what did people wear in the 90&#8217;s? I can&#8217;t remember. But they listened to The Lemonheads and Terence Trent D&#8217;Arby. And that&#8217;s what you&#8217;re about to do, you lucky person. (88 minutes)</p>
